NOTE: note_004
================================================================================

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, table_with_tabs, inconsistent_formatting
PRE-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: Bilateral hilar adenopathy, suspected sarcoidosis. (ICD: D86.0)
POST-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: Same.

PROCEDURE:

1. Flexible bronchoscopy
2. Endobronchial ultrasound with transbronchial needle aspiration (EBUS-TBNA)
3. Radial EBUS (rEBUS)
4. Transbronchial lung biopsy (TBLB)

* INDICATION: [PATIENT] is a [DOB:REDACTED] male with progressive shortness of breath and bilateral hilar fullness on recent CT chest.

** ANESTHESIA: General
** INSTRUMENTS: Olympus BF-H190, Olympus BF-UC190F, UM-S20-17S radial probe.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
The patient was placed supine. Time out completed. Following induction of GA, an i-gel was placed. The standard therapeutic bronchoscope was passed. Airway exam showed mildly edematous mucosa but no mass. The scope was exchanged for the linear EBUS.
Ultrasound survey:
Station	Size	Appearance
4R	12mm	Homogeneous
7	18mm	Hypoechoic
11L	15mm	Round
11R	14mm	Oval

We sampled Station 7 (4 passes, 21G needle). Then Station 11L (3 passes). Then Station 11R (3 passes).
We then switched back to the standard scope and advanced a radial EBUS probe into the RB3 segment where a small subsolid density was noted. Concentric signal achieved. Transbronchial forceps biopsies were obtained x5.

SPECIMENS:

* EBUS TBNA Station 7
* EBUS TBNA Station 11L
* EBUS TBNA Station 11R
* TBLB RB3

COMPLICATIONS: None. Minimal EBL. Fluoro time 0.5 mins.

PLAN: Follow up in clinic in 1 week.

NOTE: note_044
================================================================================

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, reordered_sections
IMPRESSION: Successful recanalization of the left mainstem bronchus using Nd:YAG laser.
SPECIMENS: None.
COMPLICATIONS: None.

PRE-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: Malignant airway obstruction (ICD C34.90)
PROCEDURE: Rigid bronchoscopy, Laser ablation.

INDICATION: [PATIENT], [REDACTED] female, metastatic breast cancer with left mainstem obstruction.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
Under general anesthesia with jet ventilation, a rigid bronchoscope was passed. The trachea and carina were normal. The left mainstem was 80% occluded by an exophytic, highly vascular tumor. We applied Nd:YAG laser at 30W pulsed mode to coagulate and vaporize the tumor. Carbonized debris was removed with rigid forceps. Airway patency was restored to approximately 100%. Hemostasis was excellent. No signs of perforation. Scope withdrawn safely.

NOTE: note_019
================================================================================

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, reordered_sections
IMPRESSION: Successful recanalization of the right intermediate bronchus using laser and mechanical coring.
SPECIMENS: Endobronchial biopsies of the right intermediate bronchus tumor.
COMPLICATIONS: Minimal bleeding, controlled with cold saline.

PRE-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: Malignant airway obstruction (ICD J98.09, C34.31)
PROCEDURE: Rigid bronchoscopy, Nd:YAG laser ablation, mechanical debulking.

INDICATION: [PATIENT], [REDACTED] male, squamous cell ca with post-obstructive pneumonia.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
Under general anesthesia with total intravenous anesthesia (TIVA), a size 12.0 Dumon rigid bronchoscope was passed into the trachea. The carina was sharp. The right mainstem was patent. The bronchus intermedius was completely occluded by an exophytic, fleshy tumor. We applied Nd:YAG laser at 20W continuous mode to coagulate the tumor base. Mechanical coring was then performed using the bevel of the rigid scope. Large tumor fragments were removed with rigid forceps. Airway patency was restored to approximately 80%, allowing visualization of the middle and lower lobe orifices. Copious purulent secretions were suctioned from the RLL. Hemostasis achieved. Scope withdrawn.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, table_with_tabs, inconsistent_formatting
PRE-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: RUL lung nodule, mediastinal lymphadenopathy.
POST-PROCEDURE DIAGNOSIS: Same.

PROCEDURE:

Flexible bronchoscopy

Endobronchial ultrasound with transbronchial needle aspiration (EBUS-TBNA)

Robotic-assisted navigational bronchoscopy

Mobile C-Arm Fluoroscopy

INDICATION: [PATIENT] is a [DOB:REDACTED] male with a 2.2 cm RUL nodule and enlarged station 7 node.

** ANESTHESIA: General Anesthesia with endotracheal intubation.
** INSTRUMENTS: Robotic bronchoscopy system, Linear EBUS, Mobile C-Arm.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
The patient was placed supine. Time out completed. Following induction of GA, an 8.0 ETT was placed. The linear EBUS scope was introduced first for mediastinal staging.
Station	Size	Passes
4R	8mm	0
7	19mm	4
11R	10mm	0

Station 7 was sampled x4 passes with a 21G needle. ROSE showed malignant cells.
The EBUS scope was removed. The robotic bronchoscope was then calibrated and introduced. We navigated to the RUL apical segment. Mobile C-Arm fluoroscopy was utilized to confirm the target in 3D space. The lesion was localized.
We obtained the following from the RUL target:

Needle aspiration x 3

Forceps biopsy x 5

Bronchial washing x 1

SPECIMENS:

EBUS TBNA Station 7

RUL TBNA

RUL Forceps Biopsies

RUL Washings

COMPLICATIONS: None. Minimal EBL. Fluoro time 1.2 mins.

PLAN: Extubated successfully. Transfer to PACU.

NOTE: note_035

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, reordered_sections
PLAN: Extubate and transfer to PACU. Monitor for pneumothorax with post-op CXR in 2 hours.
SPECIMENS: 1. RML nodule FNA. 2. RML nodule TBBx.
COMPLICATIONS: None.

PRE-OP DIAGNOSIS: Right middle lobe pulmonary nodule
POST-OP DIAGNOSIS: Same.

PROCEDURE:

Electromagnetic navigational bronchoscopy (31627)

Transbronchial biopsy (31628)

Fluoroscopy guidance

INDICATION: [PATIENT], [REDACTED] yr old female, with a 1.4 cm RML nodule increasing in size.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
Under general anesthesia, a flexible bronchoscope was inserted. Navigation to the RML lateral segment was successful using the pre-planned electromagnetic pathway. Fluoroscopy confirmed target location. Radial EBUS was deployed and showed a concentric view of the lesion. TBNA x3 passes performed using an aspirating needle. Subsequently, TBBx x5 using flexible forceps were obtained. The scope was removed. Patient remained hemodynamically stable throughout the procedure with no signs of bleeding.

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: extreme_length, reordered_sections
PLAN: Extubate and transfer to PACU. Monitor for pneumothorax with post-op CXR.
SPECIMENS: 1. RLL nodule BAL. 2. RLL nodule FNA. 3. RLL nodule core biopsy.
COMPLICATIONS: None.

PRE-OP DIAGNOSIS: Right lower lobe pulmonary nodule (ICD-10 R91.1)
POST-OP DIAGNOSIS: Same.

PROCEDURE:

1. Robotic-assisted navigational bronchoscopy (31627)
2. Transbronchial biopsy (31628)
3. Fluoroscopy

INDICATION: [PATIENT], [REDACTED] yr old, with a 1.8 cm RLL nodule.

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL:
Under general anesthesia, the robotic bronchoscope was calibrated and inserted. Navigation to the RLL superior segment (RB6) was successful using pre-planned pathways. Fluoroscopy confirmed target. Radial EBUS showed an eccentric view, adjusted to concentric. TBNA x3 passes performed. Then, TBBx x4 using flexible forceps. Finally, a small BAL was performed in the segment. The robotic scope was removed. Patient remained hemodynamically stable.

NOTE: note_026

NOTE TEXT:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EDGE_CASE_TAGS: missing_section, malformed_codes
PRE/POST DIAGNOSIS

Mediastinal adenopathy (R59.0)

Suspected lung cancer

PROCEDURE

Bronchoscopy with EBUS-TBNA (31620-59, 31652-)

ANESTHESIA: Moderate Sedation
MONITORING: Standard ASA

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL
[PATIENT] is a [REDACTED] year old who presents for evaluation of mediastinal lymphadenopathy. After informed consent, patient was brought to the bronchoscopy suite. A time out was performed. Under moderate sedation, a flexible bronchoscope was introduced via the mouth. Airway inspection revealed normal vocal cords, trachea, and bilateral bronchial trees. No endobronchial lesions.

The linear EBUS scope was then introduced. We surveyed stations 4R, 7, and 10R.
Station 7 measured 1.8 cm. Station 4R measured 1.4 cm.
TBNA was performed at Station 7 x3 passes, and Station 4R x3 passes using a 22G needle. Rapid on-site evaluation (ROSE) was present and showed lymphocytes.

COMPLICATIONS: None
IMPRESSION/PLAN

Successful EBUS-TBNA of 4R and 7 (two stations sampled).

Await final pathology.

MONITORING: Standard ASA

PROCEDURE IN DETAIL
[PATIENT] is a [REDACTED] year old who presents for evaluation of mediastinal lymphadenopathy. After informed consent, patient was brought to the bronchoscopy suite. A time out was performed. Under general anesthesia, a flexible bronchoscope was introduced via the ETT. Airway inspection revealed normal vocal cords, trachea, and bilateral bronchial trees. No endobronchial lesions.

The linear EBUS scope (BF-UC180F) was then introduced. We surveyed stations 4R, 4L, 7, 10R, 11L.
Station 7 measured 1.5 cm. Station 4R measured 1.2 cm.
TBNA was performed at Station 7 x4 passes, and Station 4R x3 passes using a 22G needle. Rapid on-site evaluation (ROSE) was present.

COMPLICATIONS: None
IMPRESSION/PLAN

1. Successful EBUS-TBNA of 4R and 7.
